***pijnlijk.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:pijnlijk.html>pijnlijk</a> (3322)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><a href = vnd.unilang:from.html>From</a> <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:pijn.html>pijn</a></i> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">-lijk</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective"><a href = vnd.unilang:adjective.html>Adjective</a></span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:pijnlijk.html>pijnlijk</a></strong> (<i>comparative</i> <b class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:pijnlijker.html>pijnlijker</a></b>, <i>superlative</i> <b class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:pijnlijkst.html>pijnlijkst</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>physically <a href = vnd.unilang:painful.html>painful</a>, inflicting bodily suffering</li>
<li><a href = vnd.unilang:sore.html>sore</a>, pained</li>
<li>psychologically hurtful</li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Inflection">Inflection</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>

<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Bijvoeglijk_naamwoord"><i><a href = vnd.unilang:bijvoeglijk.html>Bijvoeglijk</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:naamwoord.html>naamwoord</a></i></span></h4>

***pinata.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:pinata.html>pinata</a> (44854)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><a href = vnd.unilang:from.html>From</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:mexican.html>Mexican</a> <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Spanish_language" class="extiw" title="w:Spanish language"><a href = vnd.unilang:spanish.html>Spanish</a></a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="es">piñata</i>, <a href = vnd.unilang:from.html>from</a> <i class="Latn mention" lang="es">piña</i>, <a href = vnd.unilang:from.html>from</a> <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Latin"><a href = vnd.unilang:latin.html>Latin</a></a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">pinea</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">pinecone</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <a href = vnd.unilang:because.html>because</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:its.html>its</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:paper.html>paper</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:cover.html>cover</a> (<a href = vnd.unilang:on.html>on</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:traditional.html>traditional</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:making.html>making</a>) resembles <a href = vnd.unilang:one.html>one</a>. Alternatively <a href = vnd.unilang:from.html>from</a> <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Spanish_language" class="extiw" title="w:Spanish language"><a href = vnd.unilang:spanish.html>Spanish</a></a></span> <a href = vnd.unilang:via.html>via</a> <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Italian_language" class="extiw" title="w:Italian language">Italian</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="it">pignatta</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss"><a href = vnd.unilang:clay.html>clay</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:pot.html>pot</a></span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>,<sup id="cite_ref-1" class="reference"><a href="cite_note-1"> | 1 | </a></sup> <a href = vnd.unilang:from.html>from</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:a.html>a</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:chinese.html>Chinese</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:custom.html>custom</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:allegedly.html>allegedly</a> introduced <a href = vnd.unilang:by.html>by</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:marco.html>Marco</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:polo.html>Polo</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-2" class="reference"><a href="cite_note-2"> | 2 | </a></sup>

<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content"><a href = vnd.unilang:latin.html>Latin</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:american.html>American</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:culture.html>culture</a></span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> <a href = vnd.unilang:a.html>A</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:doll.html>doll</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:or.html>or</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:other.html>other</a> decorated <a href = vnd.unilang:container.html>container</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:that.html>that</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> filled <a href = vnd.unilang:with.html>with</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:candy.html>candy</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:and.html>and</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:hit.html>hit</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:with.html>with</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:a.html>a</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:hammer.html>hammer</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:or.html>or</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:a.html>a</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:stick.html>stick</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:by.html>by</a> blindfolded <a href = vnd.unilang:children.html>children</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:during.html>during</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:birthday.html>birthday</a> parties <a href = vnd.unilang:or.html>or</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:other.html>other</a> celebrations <a href = vnd.unilang:until.html>until</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:the.html>the</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:candy.html>candy</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:falls.html>falls</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:out.html>out</a>.</li></ol>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb"><a href = vnd.unilang:verb.html>Verb</a></span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>

<p>Borrowed <a href = vnd.unilang:from.html>from</a> <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Papiamento" class="extiw" title="w:Papiamento">Papiamentu</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="pap"><a href = vnd.unilang:pinda.html>pinda</a></i>, <a href = vnd.unilang:from.html>from</a> <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Kongo_language" class="extiw" title="w:Kongo language"><a href = vnd.unilang:kongo.html>Kongo</a></a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="kg">mpinda</i>; <head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:pingelen.html>pingelen</a> (53517)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>

<a href = vnd.unilang:if.html>if</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:so.html>so</a>, cognate <a href = vnd.unilang:with.html>with</a> <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">pinkelen</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss"><a href = vnd.unilang:pinch.html>pinch</a></span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> (<span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/English_language" class="extiw" title="w:English language"><a href = vnd.unilang:english.html>English</a></a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:pinch.html>pinch</a></i>) <a href = vnd.unilang:and.html>and</a> <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:pimpelen.html>pimpel</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss"><a href = vnd.unilang:small.html>small</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:glass.html>glass</a></span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <a href = vnd.unilang:also.html>also</a> "<a href = vnd.unilang:blue.html>blue</a> tit."
